       <div class="body" itemprop="articleBody">
        <div itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Organization">
         <meta content="Vulture" itemprop="name"/>
         <link href="http://www.vulture.com" itemprop="sameAs"/>
        </div>
        <meta content="http://www.vulture.com/2010/03/bill_murrays_latest_role_part.html" itemprop="url"/>
        <p>
         It should be obvious why Bill Murray isnt
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: Internal: vulture" href="http://www.vulture.com/2009/11/bill_murray_on_ghostbusters_3.html">
          as gung-ho
         </a>
         about a third
         <em>
          Ghostbusters
         </em>
         as the rest of the principals: Why should he waste his time on movie sets trying to reclaim past glories when he can just continue being awesome in real life? Note the below video, shot this past weekend at an Austin bar during SXSW, in which Murray matter-of-factly installs himself as an auxiliary bartender. As the understandably giddy guy doing the intro explains, Murray was doing tequila shots at the bar, left to check out some music, and then came back to pull an impromptu shift. Oh, also, he brought RZA and GZA with him, although, tragically, theyre not in the clip. (It's Jim Jarmusch's 2003 vignette-feature
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: External" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H6EZkIaJcCI">
          <em>
           Coffee and Cigarettes
          </em>
         </a>
         come to life!) Bill Murray, we salute you.
        </p>
        <iframe allowtransparency="true" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" src="http://videos.nymag.com/embed/player/?content=1GVSWS13S67PBVBG&amp;widget_type_cid=svp&amp;widget_template_cid=custom">
        </iframe>
        <p>
         <br/>
         [Via
         <a data-track="Body Text Link: External" href="http://www.gq.com/blogs/the-q/2010/03/another-reason-we-wish-wed-gone-to-sxsw-this-year-bill-murray-tending-bar.html">
          GQ
         </a>
         ]
        </p>
